-- ================================================================
--  INSTAGRAM AFFILIATE MARKETING — SAMPLE DATA
--  500 rows per table  ·  5 tables  ·  2,500 total rows
--  Compatible with MySQL 8+ / PostgreSQL 14+
--  Generated for GitHub portfolio project
-- ================================================================

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0;  -- MySQL: disable FK checks during load

-- ================================================================
-- SCHEMA (create tables if not exist)
-- ================================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS affiliate_products (
    product_id      INT PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name    VARCHAR(150),
    brand           VARCHAR(80),
    category        VARCHAR(60),
    price           DECIMAL(10,2),
    commission_rate DECIMAL(5,2)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS posts (
    post_id             INT PRIMARY KEY,
    post_date           DATETIME,
    caption             TEXT,
    media_type          VARCHAR(20),
    affiliate_product_id INT,
    hashtags            TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS post_insights (
    insight_id   INT PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id      INT,
    views        BIGINT,
    comments     INT,
    likes        INT,
    saves        INT,
    reach        INT,
    recorded_at  DATE
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS link_clicks (
    click_id     INT PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id      INT,
    click_source VARCHAR(30),
    device_type  VARCHAR(20),
    clicked_at   DATETIME,
    session_id   VARCHAR(60)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS conversions (
    conversion_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    click_id      INT,
    post_id       INT,
    sale_amount   DECIMAL(10,2),
    commission    DECIMAL(10,2),
    converted_at  DATETIME,
    status        VARCHAR(20)
);
